It’s the most natural way to write music on digital device, ever.\r\n\r\nAN ORCHESTRA IN THE TIP OF YOUR PEN\r\nStaffPad contains a bespoke playback engine, and an entire orchestra which has been meticulously recorded and programmed to play back your score with incredible realism. Use your eraser button on the pen to remove both ink strokes and existing notation.
